namespace = dg_orthodox
province_event = {
	id = dg_orthodox.001
	title = dg_orthodox.001.t
	desc = dg_orthodox.001.d
	picture = orthodox_monks
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_province_flag = lavra
		set_province_flag = anchorite_hermitage
		set_province_flag = cenobitic_monastery
		every_neighbor_province = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				every_neighbor_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								base_production = 2
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = stavropegic_monastery
						}
						OR = {
							religion = orthodox
							is_colony = yes
							has_empty_adjacent_province = yes
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = cenobitic_monastery
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.001.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_owner_religion = yes
				is_colony = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		owner = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = cenobitic_monastery
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = cenobitic_monastery
					duration = 10000
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							religion_group = christian
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = orthodox_10
					hidden_effect = {
						change_variable = {
							which = orthodox
							value = 2
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = province_religion
							value = -2
						}
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_province = {
					clr_province_flag = cenobitic_monastery
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.001.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_owner_religion = yes
				}
				is_colony = yes
				has_empty_adjacent_province = yes
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						base_production = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = anchorite_hermitage
			duration = 10000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					religion_group = christian
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = orthodox_10
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = orthodox
					value = 2
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = province_religion
					value = -2
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				every_owned_province = {
					clr_province_flag = cenobitic_monastery
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.001.c
		trigger = {
			has_owner_religion = yes
			OR = {
				is_capital = yes
				AND = {
					has_province_flag = university_present
				}
				has_province_modifier = orthodox_patriarchate
				AND = {
					base_production = 10
				}
			}
			owner = {
				religion = orthodox
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = lavra
			duration = 10000
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				every_owned_province = {
					clr_province_flag = cenobitic_monastery
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.001.f
		trigger = {
			has_owner_religion = yes
			OR = {
				is_capital = yes
				AND = {
					has_province_flag = university_present
				}
				has_province_modifier = orthodox_patriarchate
				AND = {
					base_production = 10
				}
			}
			owner = {
				religion = orthodox
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = church_property
						value = 10
					}
				}
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_modifier = orthodox_patriarchate
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = stavropegic_monastery
			duration = -1
		}
		owner = {
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_country_modifier
				religious_scandal_country_strong = {
					remove_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_strong
				}
				religious_scandal_country = {
					remove_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country
				}
				religious_scandal_country_weak = {
					remove_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_weak
				}
			}
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_country_modifier
				unhappy_church_powerful = {
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
				}
				unhappy_church_strong = {
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
				}
				unhappy_church_moderate = {
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
				}
				unhappy_church_weak = {
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
				}
				unhappy_church_impotent = {
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
				}
			}
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = church_property
					value = 1
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					clr_province_flag = cenobitic_monastery
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.001.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					manpower_percentage = 0.80
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					manpower_percentage = 1.00
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						manpower_percentage = 0.50
					}
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						manpower_percentage = 0.25
					}
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						manpower_percentage = 0.10
					}
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						manpower_percentage = 0.05
					}
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_prestige = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_prestige = -2
			}
			custom_tooltip = monastic_decline_explained
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = monastic_decline
					value = 1
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					clr_province_flag = cenobitic_monastery
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = dg_orthodox.002
	title = dg_orthodox.002.t
	desc = dg_orthodox.002.d
	picture = orthodox_hermit_meeting
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = seeking_elders_blessing
		religion = orthodox
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = ruler_pilgrimage
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				stability = 0
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			stability = 1
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_strong
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_weak
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			is_at_war = yes
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			at_war_with_religious_enemy = yes
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			war_exhaustion = 5
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			war_exhaustion = 10
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				legitimacy = 25
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				legitimacy = 50
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				legitimacy = 75
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				prestige = 0
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = religious_civil_war
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				ADM = 2
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				DIP = 2
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				MIL = 2
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			ADM = 4
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			DIP = 4
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			MIL = 4
			factor = 0.7
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = seeking_elders_blessing
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.002.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				legitimacy = 100
				NOT = {
					war_exhaustion = 2
				}
				stability = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				legitimacy = 100
				NOT = {
					war_exhaustion = 2
				}
				NOT = {
					stability = 0
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				random = {
					chance = 40
					custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
					hidden_effect = {
						change_variable = {
							which = stability_points
							value = 50
						}
						country_event = {
							id = POP_Stability.002
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				random = {
					chance = 30
					custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
					hidden_effect = {
						change_variable = {
							which = stability_points
							value = 50
						}
						country_event = {
							id = POP_Stability.002
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				random = {
					chance = 20
					custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
					hidden_effect = {
						change_variable = {
							which = stability_points
							value = 50
						}
						country_event = {
							id = POP_Stability.002
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				random = {
					chance = 10
					custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
					hidden_effect = {
						change_variable = {
							which = stability_points
							value = 50
						}
						country_event = {
							id = POP_Stability.002
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				legitimacy = 100
				war_exhaustion = 2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_war_exhaustion = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_war_exhaustion = -3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_war_exhaustion = -2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_war_exhaustion = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					legitimacy = 100
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = 6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = 4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.002.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				advisor = theologian
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_treasury = -1
		if = {
			limit = {
				legitimacy = 100
				NOT = {
					war_exhaustion = 2
				}
				stability = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				legitimacy = 100
				NOT = {
					war_exhaustion = 2
				}
				NOT = {
					stability = 0
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				random = {
					chance = 40
					custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
					hidden_effect = {
						change_variable = {
							which = stability_points
							value = 50
						}
						country_event = {
							id = POP_Stability.002
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				random = {
					chance = 30
					custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
					hidden_effect = {
						change_variable = {
							which = stability_points
							value = 50
						}
						country_event = {
							id = POP_Stability.002
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				random = {
					chance = 20
					custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
					hidden_effect = {
						change_variable = {
							which = stability_points
							value = 50
						}
						country_event = {
							id = POP_Stability.002
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {

				}

			}

country_event = {
	id = dg_orthodox.003
	title = dg_orthodox.003.t
	desc = dg_orthodox.003.d
	picture = orthodox_hermit
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = seeking_elders_blessing
		religion = orthodox
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = ruler_pilgrimage
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3
	}
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = seeking_elders_blessing
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.003.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					legitimacy = 100
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					legitimacy = 75
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					legitimacy = 50
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					legitimacy = 25
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_country_strong
				duration = 400
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_country
				duration = 400
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_country_weak
				duration = 400
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_country_weak
				duration = 400
			}
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = anchorite_hermitage
			}
			remove_province_modifier = anchorite_hermitage
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_province
				duration = 1000
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.003.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_prestige = -4
			add_legitimacy = -8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_prestige = -3
			add_legitimacy = -6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {

province_event = {
	id = dg_orthodox.012
	title = dg_orthodox.012.t
	desc = dg_orthodox.012.d
	picture = orthodox_iconoclasm
	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = religious_icon
		controller = {
			NOT = {
				religion = orthodox
			}
			NOT = {
				religion = catholic
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.012.a
		remove_province_modifier = religious_icon
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_province
				duration = 2000
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_province
				duration = 1000
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_province
				duration = 500
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_province
				duration = 250
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					religion = orthodox
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.60
					}
					add_prestige = -8
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = morale_boost
						duration = 200
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.20
					}
					add_prestige = -6
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = morale_boost
						duration = 150
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
					add_prestige = -4
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = morale_boost
						duration = 100
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.60
					}
					add_prestige = -2
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = morale_boost
						duration = 50
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = dg_orthodox.013
	title = ai_only.t
	desc = ai_only.d
	picture = ai_only
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		religion = orthodox
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = orthodox_timer
		}
		piety = -0.60
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 25
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = orthodox_timer

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_province = {
					religion = orthodox

					}

						has_province_modifier = stavropegic_monastery
					}

						has_province_modifier = anchorite_hermitage

						has_province_modifier = monastic_town
					}

						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = lavra

							NOT = {
								any_owned_province = {
									has_province_modifier = religious_icon
								}
							}
						}
					}
					controlled_by = owner
					has_siege = no
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = orthodox_event
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					religion = orthodox
					is_city = yes
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = cenobitic_monastery
					}
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = stavropegic_monastery
					}
					NOT = {

				}

			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_only.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = orthodox_event
				has_country_flag = great_schism

						has_province_flag = old_believers
					}

					is_city = yes
				}
				NOT = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_province_modifier = religious_nationalism
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				clr_country_flag = orthodox_event
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = old_believers
						}
						religion = orthodox
						is_in_capital_area = yes
						is_city = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {

								}
							}

							}
						}
					}

						}
					}
					if = {

							}

						}
					}

province_event = {
	id = dg_orthodox.014
	title = dg_orthodox.014.t
	desc = dg_orthodox.014.d
	picture = orthodox_icon
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			province_id = 359
		}
		owner = {
			OR = {
				religion = orthodox

						}

						}

					name = heretic_minority_6

country_event = {
	id = dg_orthodox.024
	title = dg_orthodox.024.t
	desc = dg_orthodox.024.d
	picture = orthodox_metropolitan
	trigger = {
		religion = orthodox
		NOT = {
			government = theocracy
		}
		NOT = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_modifier = orthodox_patriarchate
			}
		}
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = orthodox_archbishopric
				has_province_modifier = orthodox_pentarchy
			}
		}
		AND = {
			OR = {
				is_subject = no
				is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
				is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 5
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = orthodox_patriarchate
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = patriarchate_seat
					value = 1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_owner_culture = yes
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = patriarchate_seat
						value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						culture_group = owner
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = patriarchate_seat
						value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_core = owner
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = patriarchate_seat
						value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_capital_area = yes
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = patriarchate_seat
						value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_overseas = yes
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = patriarchate_seat
						value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_capital = yes
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = patriarchate_seat
						value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = patriarchate_seat
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.024.a
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = orthodox_patriarchate
				all_province = {
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = patriarchate_seat
								which = PREV
							}
						}
						is_variable_equal = {
							which = patriarchate_seat
							which = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			remove_province_modifier = orthodox_archbishopric
			remove_province_modifier = orthodox_pentarchy
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = orthodox_patriarchate
				duration = -1
			}
			province_event = {
				id = dg_orthodox.026
				days = 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				set_variable = {
					which = patriarchate_seat
					value = 0
				}
			}

			limit = {
				FROM = {
					total_development = 150
				}
			}
			add_prestige = 1
		}

		name = dg_orthodox.027.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {

				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = appointed_metropolitan
			}
			set_country_flag = patriarch_appointed
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient

						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
						patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_observant
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_country_modifier
					patriarch_hostile_observant = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
					}
					patriarch_hostile_pious = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
					}
					patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_country_modifier
				patriarch_hostile_observant = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
				}
				patriarch_hostile_pious = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
				}
				patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

						}

				}

							total_development = 35
						}

					add_prestige = 4
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {

							total_development = 15
						}
					}
					add_prestige = 3
				}
				else_if = {

							total_development = 8
						}
					}
					add_prestige = 2
				}
				else = {
					add_prestige = 1
				}
			}
			if = {

					FROM = {
						has_country_flag = send_tribute_to_patriarch
					}

				reverse_add_opinion = {
					who = FROM

				}

				}

						}

					add_prestige = 8
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							total_development = 15
						}
					}
					add_prestige = 6
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							total_development = 8
						}
					}

				}

					add_prestige = 2
				}
				FROM = {
					clr_country_flag = send_tribute_to_patriarch
				}
			}
		}
	}

		add_stability = -1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = POP_Stability.003
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_emperor_of_china = yes
			}
			add_mandate = -5
		}
		every_known_country = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					religion = catholic
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.60
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = changed_religion_pious
					}
					add_casus_belli = {
						target = ROOT
						type = cb_insult
						months = 24
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.20
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = changed_religion_observant
					}
					add_casus_belli = {
						target = ROOT
						type = cb_insult
						months = 12
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = changed_religion_decadent
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			else_if = {
				limit = {

				}

						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_observant
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_country_modifier
					patriarch_hostile_observant = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
					}
					patriarch_hostile_pious = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
					}
					patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {

				on_trigger = has_country_modifier

				}

						piety = 0.60
					}
					add_prestige = -10
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.20
					}
					add_prestige = -8
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
					add_prestige = -6
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.60
					}
					add_prestige = -4
				}
				else = {
					add_prestige = -2
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			every_known_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = orthodox
					any_owned_province = {
						has_province_modifier = orthodox_patriarchate
					}
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
				add_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = rejected_patriarch_authority
				}
			}
		}
	}

							name = patriarch_corrupt_pious
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						patriarch_authority = 0.10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
							}
						}
						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_country_modifier
							patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
							}
							patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
							}
						}
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = patriarch_corrupt_observant
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_corrupt_observant = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
						}
						patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
						}
						patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_country_modifier
					patriarch_corrupt_observant = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
					}
					patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
					}
					patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						patriarch_authority = 0.75
					}

							}

						}

							duration = -1
						}
					}

					}

							}
						}

							}
							patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {

							}
						}

							duration = -1
						}
					}

				else_if = {

province_event = {
	id = dg_orthodox.074
	title = dg_orthodox.074.t
	desc = dg_orthodox.074.d
	picture = orthodox_patriarch_migration
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = patriarch_resistance
		OR = {
			owner = {
				religion = orthodox
			}
			owner = {
				religion = coptic
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = patriarch_resistance_dip
			}
			custom_tooltip = patriarch_resistance_dip
			owner = {
				add_years_of_income = 0.04
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = patriarch_resistance_adm
			}
			custom_tooltip = patriarch_resistance_adm
			owner = {
				remove_country_modifier = religious_tolerance
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = patriarch_resistance_exc
			}
			custom_tooltip = patriarch_resistance_exc
			clr_province_flag = patriarch_resistance_exc
			owner = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.60
					}
					add_prestige = -5
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.20
					}
					add_prestige = -4
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
					add_prestige = -3
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.60
					}
					add_prestige = -2
				}
				else = {
					add_prestige = -1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = patriarch_resistance_mil
			}
			custom_tooltip = patriarch_resistance_mil
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						province_id = 2530
					}
				}
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = catholic_rebels
					size = 1
					win = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							province_id = 2530
						}
					}
					owner = {
						religion = orthodox
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = union_of_churches
						}
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = support_miaphysite_union
						}
					}
				}
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = coptic_rebels
					size = 1
					win = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							province_id = 2530
						}
					}
					owner = {
						religion = coptic
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = union_of_churches
						}
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = support_miaphysite_union
						}
					}

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_prestige = -10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_prestige = -8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_prestige = -6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_prestige = -4
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		clr_country_flag = religious_turmoil_orthodox
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = religious_tolerance
				duration = 1000
			}
			add_piety = -0.20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance
			}
			remove_country_modifier = religious_intolerance
			add_piety = -0.20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_province = {
					religion = orthodox
					has_missionary = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					religion = orthodox
					has_missionary = yes
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = missionary_failure
					duration = 3000
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = patriarch_protest
				}
				clr_province_flag = patriarch_protest
				set_variable = {
					which = patriarch_influence
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.081.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_adm_power = -5
		custom_tooltip = puppet_patriarch_explained
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = orthodox_patriarch_timer
			duration = 3000
			hidden = yes
		}
		random = {
			chance = 30
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = patriarch_protest
				}
				remove_province_modifier = orthodox_patriarchate_captive
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = orthodox_patriarchate_vacant
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = patriarch_protest
				}
				clr_province_flag = patriarch_protest
				set_variable = {
					which = patriarch_influence
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.081.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = christians_permitted
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = christians_tolerated
			}
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = patriarch_protest
			}
			remove_province_modifier = orthodox_patriarchate_captive
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = patriarch_influence
						value = 25
					}
				}
				owner = {
					add_treasury = 250
				}
				add_nationalism = 10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = patriarch_influence
						value = 16
					}
				}
				owner = {
					add_treasury = 200
				}
				add_nationalism = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = patriarch_influence
						value = 9
					}
				}
				owner = {
					add_treasury = 150
				}
				add_nationalism = 6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = patriarch_influence
						value = 4
					}
				}
				owner = {
					add_treasury = 100
				}
				add_nationalism = 4
			}
			else = {
				owner = {
					add_treasury = 50
				}
				add_nationalism = 2
			}
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = orthodox_patriarchate_vacant
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = patriarch_protest
				}
				clr_province_flag = patriarch_protest
				set_variable = {
					which = patriarch_influence
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}

					NOT = {
						has_province_flag = orthodox_patriarchate
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = patriarch_flight
					value = 1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						culture_group = ROOT
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = patriarch_flight
						value = 2
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						culture = ROOT
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = patriarch_flight
						value = 2
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						religion = orthodox
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = patriarch_flight
						value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = orthodox_patriarch_of_jerusalem
					}
					set_variable = {
						which = patriarch_flight
						value = 0
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_province = {
								province_id = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						which = patriarch_flight
						value = 0
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							ai = no
							has_country_flag = returned_patriarch_to_bondage
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						which = patriarch_flight
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.06.a
		random_province = {
			limit = {
				all_province = {
					province_group = antioch_patriarch_area
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = patriarch_flight
								which = PREV
							}
						}
						is_variable_equal = {
							which = patriarch_flight
							which = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			province_event = {
				id = dg_orthodox.083
				days = 30
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_province = {
				set_variable = {
					which = patriarch_flight
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
